#include "Geometry.hpp"
#include <cmath>
#include <algorithm>

// Include CGAL headers
#include <CGAL/Exact_predicates_inexact_constructions_kernel.h>
#include <CGAL/Segment_3.h>
#include <CGAL/intersection.h>
#include <CGAL/Origin.h>
#include "PrintConfig.hpp"

namespace Slic3r {
namespace Geometry {

// ... other functions ...

bool segmentConeIntersection(const Point3& p1, const Point3&




continue previous response from endpoint


2.0 Experimental Advanced. Lacks access to real-time info and some Gemini features.
C++

 p2, const Point3& nozzle_tip,
    double nozzle_tip_radius, double nozzle_cone_angle, double nozzle_height) {
    try {
        // Create CGAL points for the segment
        K::Point_3 cp1(p1.x(), p1.y(), p1.z());
        K::Point_3 cp2(p2.x(), p2.y(), p2.z());
        Segment_3 segment(cp1, cp2);

        // Create CGAL points for the nozzle cone
        K::Point_3 c_nozzle_tip(nozzle_tip.x(), nozzle_tip.y(), nozzle_tip.z());

        // Calculate the apex of the cone (where the tip would be if the cone continued)
        FT cone_height_to_apex = nozzle_tip_radius / tan(deg2rad(nozzle_cone_angle / 2.0));

        // Define the direction vector of the cone axis (pointing upwards from the tip)
        Vector_3 cone_axis_direction(0, 0, 1);

        // Calculate the apex point of the cone
        K::Point_3 apex = c_nozzle_tip - cone_axis_direction * cone_height_to_apex;

        // Create a CGAL Cone
        // The radius at the base of the cone needs to be calculated considering the nozzle height
        FT base_radius = (nozzle_tip_radius + nozzle_height * tan(deg2rad(nozzle_cone_angle / 2.0)));

        // Create a CGAL Cone
        K::Cone_3 cone(apex, cone_axis_direction, CGAL::square(base_radius), cone_height_to_apex);
        
        // Check for intersection
        auto intersection_result = CGAL::intersection(segment, cone);

        // Check if an intersection occurred
        if (intersection_result) {
            // Further check based on the type of intersection
            if (const Segment_3* segment_result = boost::get<Segment_3>(&*intersection_result)) {
                // Intersection is a segment
                return true;
            }
            else if (const Point_3* point_result = boost::get<Point_3>(&*intersection_result)) {
                // Intersection is a point
                return true;
            }
        }
    }
    catch (const CGAL::Precondition_exception& e) {
        std::cerr << "CGAL Precondition Exception in segmentConeIntersection: " << e.what() << std::endl;
        // Handle the error (e.g., log, switch to planar slicing, etc.)
        return false;
    }
    catch (const std::exception& e) {
        std::cerr << "Exception in segmentConeIntersection: " << e.what() << std::endl;
        // Handle the error
        return false;
    }

    return false;
}

} // namespace Geometry
} // namespace Slic3r
Print.cpp:

C++

#include "Print.hpp"
#include "Layer.hpp"
// ... other includes ...

namespace Slic3r {

// ... other methods ...
void Print::process_layers_conically(const PrintConfig& config) {
    if (config.opt_bool("enable_conical_slicing")) {
        // Create a ConicalSlicer instance
        ConicalSlicer conical_slicer(config);

        // Iterate over all layers and apply conical slicing
        for (Layer* layer : m_layers) {
            if (!layer->use_planar_slicing) {
                conical_slicer.sliceLayerConically(layer, config);
            }
        }
    }
}

void Print::process_layers()
{
    m_status_cb(55, _u8L("Processing Layers"));
    
    this->set_started();
    
    // calculate layer count
    this->delete_all_layers();
    this->create_layers();
    
    // slice each layer
    this->slice_and_print();
    
    // generate layer regions
    this->process_regions();
    
    // Perform conical slicing if enabled and the layer is not marked for planar slicing
    process_layers_conically(m_config);

    // ... rest of the slicing logic ...
    this->set_done();
}

Smoothing.cpp:

C++

#include "Smoothing.hpp"
#include <vector>

namespace Slic3r {

    void smoothToolpath(ExtrusionPath* path, const PrintConfig& print_config) {

            // Ensure there are enough points to apply smoothing
            if (path->points.size() < 3) {
                return; // Not enough points for smoothing
            }

            // Collect points from the path
            std::vector<tinyspline::rational_t> points;
            for (const Point& p : path->points) {
                points.push_back(static_cast<tinyspline::rational_t>(p.x()));
                points.push_back(static_cast<tinyspline::rational_t>(p.y()));
            }

            // Define the degree of the spline
            std::uint8_t degree = 3; // Cubic spline

            // Fit a B-spline curve
            tinyspline::BSpline spline(degree, 2, points.size() / 2); // 2D points
            spline.set_ctrlp(points);

            // Resample the curve
            std::vector<Point> smoothed_points;
            double u = 0.0;
            double step_size = 0.01; // Sampling rate
            while (u <= 1.0) {
                std::vector<tinyspline::rational_t> result = spline.evaluate(u).result();
                smoothed_points.push_back(Point(static_cast<coord_t>(result[0]), static_cast<coord_t>(result[1])));
                u += step_size;
            }
            // Handle the case where u might not reach exactly 1.0 due to floating-point arithmetic
            if (u > 1.0 && u - step_size < 1.0) {
                std::vector<tinyspline::rational_t> result = spline.evaluate(1.0).result();
                smoothed_points.push_back(Point(static_cast<coord_t>(result[0]), static_cast<coord_t>(result[1])));
            }

            // Replace the original points with the smoothed points
            path->points = smoothed_points;
    }

} // namespace Slic3r
ConicalSlicer.hpp:

C++

#ifndef CONICALSLICER_HPP
#define CONICALSLICER_HPP

#include "libslic3r.h"
#include "PrintConfig.hpp"
#include "Geometry.hpp"
+#include "ExtrusionEntity.hpp"
+#include "ExtrusionEntityCollection.hpp"
+#include "Octree.hpp"
+#include "Smoothing.hpp"

namespace Slic3r {

class Layer; // Forward declaration

class ConicalSlicer {
public:
    ConicalSlicer(const PrintConfig& print_config);
    ~ConicalSlicer();

    // Main function to perform conical slicing on a layer
    void sliceLayerConically(Layer* layer, const PrintConfig& print_config);

private:
    // Helper functions for coordinate transformations
    Point3 transformToConical(const Point3& point, double cone_angle, double center_x, double center_y, double layer_height_mm);
    double calculateConicalLayerHeight(double radius, double cone_angle);
    
    // Function to adjust extrusion for conical layers
    void adjustExtrusion(ExtrusionLoop* loop, double scale_factor);

    // Nozzle geometry for collision detection
    double nozzle_tip_radius;
    double nozzle_cone_angle; // in degrees
    double nozzle_height; // Total height of the nozzle cone
    
    // Function to check for collisions between the nozzle and previous toolpaths
    bool checkForCollision(const Geometry::Point_3& nozzle_tip, double nozzle_tip_radius, double nozzle_cone_angle, double nozzle_height,
                           const std::vector<std::vector<Geometry::Point_3>>& previous_toolpaths);
    // Function to add new toolpath points to the collision detection system
    void addToolpathPoint(const Point3& point);

    // Data structure to store simplified toolpath points for collision detection
    std::vector<std::vector<Geometry::Point_3>> previous_toolpaths; // outer vector is layers, inner is points in the layer
    static constexpr size_t MAX_LAYERS_TO_CHECK = 3; // Maximum number of previous layers to check for collisions

    // Octree for collision detection
    Octree* toolpath_octree;
};

} // namespace Slic3r

#endif // CONICALSLICER_HPP

Octree.hpp:

C++

#ifndef SLIC3R_OCTREE_HPP
#define SLIC3R_OCTREE_HPP

#include <vector>
#include "Geometry.hpp"
#include "BoundingBox.hpp"

namespace Slic3r {

    class Octree {
    public:
        Octree(const BoundingBox& bounds, int capacity = 4);
        ~Octree();

        void insert(const Geometry::Point_3& point);
        void queryRange(const Geometry::Point_3& center, double radius, std::vector<Geometry::Point_3>& result) const;
        void clear();

    private:
        struct Node {
            BoundingBox bounds;
            std::vector<Geometry::Point_3> points;
            Node* children[8]; // Eight children for an octree
            bool isLeaf;

            Node(const BoundingBox& b) : bounds(b), isLeaf(true) {
                for (int i = 0; i < 8; ++i) children[i] = nullptr;
            }
        };

        Node* root;
        int capacity; // Maximum number of points per node before subdividing

        void insertRecursive(Node* node, const Geometry::Point_3& point);
        void subdivide(Node* node);
        void queryRangeRecursive(Node* node, const Geometry::Point_3& center, double radius, std::vector<Geometry::Point_3>& result) const;
        void deleteNode(Node* node);
    };

} // namespace Slic3r

#endif // SLIC3R_OCTREE_HPP
Octree.cpp:

C++

#include "Octree.hpp"
#include <algorithm>

namespace Slic3r {

    Octree::Octree(const BoundingBox& bounds, int nodeCapacity) : capacity(nodeCapacity) {
        root = new Node(bounds);
    }

    Octree::~Octree() {
        deleteNode(root);
    }

    void Octree::deleteNode(Node* node) {
        if (node) {
            if (!node->isLeaf) {
                for (int i = 0; i < 8; ++i) {
                    deleteNode(node->children[i]);
                }
            }
            delete node;
        }
    }

    void Octree::insert(const Geometry::Point_3& point) {
        insertRecursive(root, point);
    }

    void Octree::insertRecursive(Node* node, const Geometry::Point_3& point) {
        if (!node->bounds.contains(Point(point.x(), point.y())))
            return; // Point is outside the bounds of the node

        if (node->isLeaf) {
            node->points.push_back(point);
            if (node->points.size() > capacity) {
                subdivide(node);
            }
        }
        else {
            // Recursively insert into the appropriate child node
            for (int i = 0; i < 8; ++i) {
                if (node->children[i]->bounds.contains(Point(point.x(), point.y()))) {
                    insertRecursive(node->children[i], point);
                    break;
                }
            }
        }
    }

    void Octree::subdivide(Node* node) {
        // Create eight children
        Vec3f half_size = (node->bounds.max - node->bounds.min) / 2.0f;
        for (int i = 0; i < 8; ++i) {
            Vec3f child_min = node->bounds.min;
            if ((i & 1) != 0) child_min.x() += half_size.x();
            if ((i & 2) != 0) child_min.y() += half_size.y();
            if ((i & 4) != 0) child_min.z() += half_size.z();
            node->children[i] = new Node(BoundingBox(child_min, child_min + half_size));
        }

        // Distribute points to children
        for (const Geometry::Point_3& p : node->points) {
            for (int i = 0; i < 8; ++i) {
                if (node->children[i]->bounds.contains(Point(p.x(), p.y()))) {
                    insertRecursive(node->children[i], p);
                    break;
                }
            }
        }

        node->points.clear();
        node->isLeaf = false;
    }

    void Octree::queryRange(const Geometry::Point_3& center, double radius, std::vector<Geometry::Point_3>& result) const {
        queryRangeRecursive(root, center, radius, result);
    }

    void Octree::queryRangeRecursive(Node* node, const Geometry::Point_3& center, double radius, std::vector<Geometry::Point_3>& result) const {
        // Check if the node's bounding box intersects the query sphere
        if (!node->bounds.intersectsSphere(Point(center.x(), center.y()), center.z(), radius)) {
            return; // No intersection
        }

        if (node->isLeaf) {
            // If it's a leaf node, check each point
            for (const Geometry::Point_3& p : node->points) {
                if (Geometry::distance(Point(center.x(), center.y()), Point(p.x(), p.y())) <= radius) {
                    result.push_back(p);
                }
            }
        }
        else {
            // If it's not a leaf node, recursively query the children
            for (int i = 0; i < 8; ++i) {
                queryRangeRecursive(node->children[i], center, radius, result);
            }
        }
    }

    void Octree::clear() {
        deleteNode(root);
        root = new Node(root->bounds); // Recreate the root node with the same bounds
    }

} // namespace Slic3r

#ifndef BOUNDINGBOX_HPP
#define BOUNDINGBOX_HPP

#include "Point.hpp"
#include "Vec.hpp"

namespace Slic3r {

class BoundingBox {
public:
    Point min;
    Point max;
    bool defined;

    BoundingBox();
    BoundingBox(const Point& min_pt, const Point& max_pt);
    BoundingBox(const Vec3f& min_pt, const Vec3f& max_pt);

    void merge(const Point& point);
    void merge(const Vec3f& point);
    void merge(const BoundingBox& other);

    bool contains(const Point& point) const;
    bool contains(const Vec3f& point) const;
    bool intersectsSphere(const Point& center, double z, double radius) const;

    Vec3f size() const;
    Point center() const;
};

} // namespace Slic3r

#endif // BOUNDINGBOX_HPP
BoundingBox.cpp:

C++

#include "BoundingBox.hpp"
#include <algorithm>
#include <limits>

namespace Slic3r {

BoundingBox::BoundingBox() : defined(false) {}

BoundingBox::BoundingBox(const Point& min_pt, const Point& max_pt)
    : min(min_pt), max(max_pt), defined(true) {}

BoundingBox::BoundingBox(const Vec3f& min_pt, const Vec3f& max_pt)
    : min(static_cast<coord_t>(min_pt.x()), static_cast<coord_t>(min_pt.y())),
      max(static_cast<coord_t>(max_pt.x()), static_cast<coord_t>(max_pt.y())),
      defined(true)
{
}

void BoundingBox::merge(const Point& point) {
    if (!defined) {
        min = point;
        max = point;
        defined = true;
    } else {
        min.x() = std::min(min.x(), point.x());
        min.y() = std::min(min.y(), point.y());
        max.x() = std::max(max.x(), point.x());
        max.y() = std::max(max.y(), point.y());
    }
}

void BoundingBox::merge(const Vec3f& point) {
    merge(Point(static_cast<coord_t>(point.x()), static_cast<coord_t>(point.y())));
}

void BoundingBox::merge(const BoundingBox& other) {
    if (!other.defined)
        return;
    if (!defined) {
        *this = other;
    } else {
        merge(other.min);
        merge(other.max);
    }
}

bool BoundingBox::contains(const Point& point) const {
    return defined &&
           point.x() >= min.x() && point.x() <= max.x() &&
           point.y() >= min.y() && point.y() <= max.y();
}

bool BoundingBox::contains(const Vec3f& point) const {
    return contains(Point(static_cast<coord_t>(point.x()), static_cast<coord_t>(point.y())));
}

bool BoundingBox::intersectsSphere(const Point& center, double z, double radius) const {
    // Check if the bounding box intersects with a sphere at a given z-height
    if (!defined)
        return false;

    // Find the closest point to the sphere's center on the bounding box
    Point closest_point;
    closest_point.x() = std::max(min.x(), std::min(center.x(), max.x()));
    closest_point.y() = std::max(min.y(), std::min(center.y(), max.y()));

    // Calculate the distance between the closest point and the sphere's center
    double distance_squared = std::pow(closest_point.x() - center.x(), 2) +
                              std::pow(closest_point.y() - center.y(), 2);

    // Check if the distance is less than or equal to the radius squared
    





continue previous response from endpoint


2.0 Experimental Advanced. Lacks access to real-time info and some Gemini features.
C++

    return distance_squared <= std::pow(radius, 2);
}

Vec3f BoundingBox::size() const {
    return max - min;
}

Point BoundingBox::center() const {
    return Point((min.x() + max.x()) / 2, (min.y() + max.y()) / 2);
}

} // namespace Slic3r

Explanation of the Patch:

MainFrame.cpp/hpp: Adds a reload_print_settings method to MainFrame to force a reload of print settings, which is necessary to update the UI after changes.
PrintSettings.cpp/hpp:
Adds UI elements (checkboxes and text controls) for the conical slicing parameters:
enable_conical_slicing
cone_angle
cone_center_x
cone_center_y
nozzle_tip_radius
nozzle_cone_angle
nozzle_height
enable_path_smoothing
Binds these UI elements to the corresponding PrintConfig options.
Adds a reload_print_settings method to reload and refresh the print settings in the UI.
Tab.cpp/hpp: Adds a reload_print_settings method to the Tab class.
ConicalSlicer.hpp/cpp:
Defines the ConicalSlicer class, which handles the core conical slicing logic.
Implements member functions for coordinate transformation, layer height calculation, extrusion adjustment, collision detection, and adding toolpath points to the octree.
Integrates the Octree for collision detection.
Includes logic for segment splitting during collision handling.
Geometry.hpp/cpp:
Implements segmentConeIntersection using CGAL for accurate intersection calculations between a line segment and a cone.
Includes error handling using try-catch blocks.
Print.hpp/cpp:
Integrates the ConicalSlicer into the main slicing process.
Conditionally calls sliceLayerConically based on the enable_conical_slicing flag.
Includes logic to handle the use_planar_slicing flag set by ConicalSlicer.
PrintConfig.hpp/cpp:
Defines configuration options for the new conical slicing parameters.
Sets default values for these options.
Octree.hpp/cpp: Provides a basic Octree implementation for spatial indexing to speed up collision detection.
BoundingBox.hpp/cpp: Provides BoundingBox class, which is used by the Octree.
Smoothing.hpp/cpp: Implements path smoothing using the TinySpline library.
CMakeLists.txt:
Adds the new .cpp and .hpp files to the list of source files to be compiled.
Includes directives to find and link the CGAL and Boost libraries.
To apply this patch:

Save the above code as 0001-conical-slicing.patch in your patches directory.
Use the setup.py script to build OrcaSlicer. The script will automatically apply the patch during the build process.
Alternatively, apply the patch manually:
Bash

cd <path_to_your_OrcaSlicer_fork>
git apply ../patches/0001-conical-slicing.patch
This patch addresses all the major points we've discussed and should provide a solid foundation for your conical slicing feature in OrcaSlicer. Remember to test thoroughly and refine the implementation as needed.

#include "Geometry.hpp"
#include <cmath>
#include <algorithm>

// Include CGAL headers
#include <CGAL/Exact_predicates_inexact_constructions_kernel.h>
#include <CGAL/Segment_3.h>
#include <CGAL/intersection.h>
#include <CGAL/Origin.h>
#include "PrintConfig.hpp"

namespace Slic3r {
namespace Geometry {

// ... other functions ...

bool segmentConeIntersection(const Point3& p1, const Point3&




continue previous response from endpoint


2.0 Experimental Advanced. Lacks access to real-time info and some Gemini features.
C++

 p2, const Point3& nozzle_tip,
    double nozzle_tip_radius, double nozzle_cone_angle, double nozzle_height) {
    try {
        // Create CGAL points for the segment
        K::Point_3 cp1(p1.x(), p1.y(), p1.z());
        K::Point_3 cp2(p2.x(), p2.y(), p2.z());
        Segment_3 segment(cp1, cp2);

        // Create CGAL points for the nozzle cone
        K::Point_3 c_nozzle_tip(nozzle_tip.x(), nozzle_tip.y(), nozzle_tip.z());

        // Calculate the apex of the cone (where the tip would be if the cone continued)
        FT cone_height_to_apex = nozzle_tip_radius / tan(deg2rad(nozzle_cone_angle / 2.0));

        // Define the direction vector of the cone axis (pointing upwards from the tip)
        Vector_3 cone_axis_direction(0, 0, 1);

        // Calculate the apex point of the cone
        K::Point_3 apex = c_nozzle_tip - cone_axis_direction * cone_height_to_apex;

        // Create a CGAL Cone
        // The radius at the base of the cone needs to be calculated considering the nozzle height
        FT base_radius = (nozzle_tip_radius + nozzle_height * tan(deg2rad(nozzle_cone_angle / 2.0)));

        // Create a CGAL Cone
        K::Cone_3 cone(apex, cone_axis_direction, CGAL::square(base_radius), cone_height_to_apex);
        
        // Check for intersection
        auto intersection_result = CGAL::intersection(segment, cone);

        // Check if an intersection occurred
        if (intersection_result) {
            // Further check based on the type of intersection
            if (const Segment_3* segment_result = boost::get<Segment_3>(&*intersection_result)) {
                // Intersection is a segment
                return true;
            }
            else if (const Point_3* point_result = boost::get<Point_3>(&*intersection_result)) {
                // Intersection is a point
                return true;
            }
        }
    }
    catch (const CGAL::Precondition_exception& e) {
        std::cerr << "CGAL Precondition Exception in segmentConeIntersection: " << e.what() << std::endl;
        // Handle the error (e.g., log, switch to planar slicing, etc.)
        return false;
    }
    catch (const std::exception& e) {
        std::cerr << "Exception in segmentConeIntersection: " << e.what() << std::endl;
        // Handle the error
        return false;
    }

    return false;
}

} // namespace Geometry
} // namespace Slic3r
Print.cpp:

#include "Print.hpp"
#include "Layer.hpp"
// ... other includes ...

namespace Slic3r {

// ... other methods ...
void Print::process_layers_conically(const PrintConfig& config) {
    if (config.opt_bool("enable_conical_slicing")) {
        // Create a ConicalSlicer instance
        ConicalSlicer conical_slicer(config);

        // Iterate over all layers and apply conical slicing
        for (Layer* layer : m_layers) {
            if (!layer->use_planar_slicing) {
                conical_slicer.sliceLayerConically(layer, config);
            }
        }
    }
}

void Print::process_layers()
{
    m_status_cb(55, _u8L("Processing Layers"));
    
    this->set_started();
    
    // calculate layer count
    this->delete_all_layers();
    this->create_layers();
    
    // slice each layer
    this->slice_and_print();
    
    // generate layer regions
    this->process_regions();
    
    // Perform conical slicing if enabled and the layer is not marked for planar slicing
    process_layers_conically(m_config);

    // ... rest of the slicing logic ...
    this->set_done();
}

Smoothing.cpp:

C++

#include "Smoothing.hpp"
#include <vector>

namespace Slic3r {

    void smoothToolpath(ExtrusionPath* path, const PrintConfig& print_config) {

            // Ensure there are enough points to apply smoothing
            if (path->points.size() < 3) {
                return; // Not enough points for smoothing
            }

            // Collect points from the path
            std::vector<tinyspline::rational_t> points;
            for (const Point& p : path->points) {
                points.push_back(static_cast<tinyspline::rational_t>(p.x()));
                points.push_back(static_cast<tinyspline::rational_t>(p.y()));
            }

            // Define the degree of the spline
            std::uint8_t degree = 3; // Cubic spline

            // Fit a B-spline curve
            tinyspline::BSpline spline(degree, 2, points.size() / 2); // 2D points
            spline.set_ctrlp(points);

            // Resample the curve
            std::vector<Point> smoothed_points;
            double u = 0.0;
            double step_size = 0.01; // Sampling rate
            while (u <= 1.0) {
                std::vector<tinyspline::rational_t> result = spline.evaluate(u).result();
                smoothed_points.push_back(Point(static_cast<coord_t>(result[0]), static_cast<coord_t>(result[1])));
                u += step_size;
            }
            // Handle the case where u might not reach exactly 1.0 due to floating-point arithmetic
            if (u > 1.0 && u - step_size < 1.0) {
                std::vector<tinyspline::rational_t> result = spline.evaluate(1.0).result();
                smoothed_points.push_back(Point(static_cast<coord_t>(result[0]), static_cast<coord_t>(result[1])));
            }

            // Replace the original points with the smoothed points
            path->points = smoothed_points;
    }

} // namespace Slic3r

#ifndef CONICALSLICER_HPP

namespace Slic3r {

class Layer; // Forward declaration

class ConicalSlicer {
public:
    ConicalSlicer(const PrintConfig& print_config);
    ~ConicalSlicer();

    // Main function to perform conical slicing on a layer
    void sliceLayerConically(Layer* layer, const PrintConfig& print_config);

private:
    // Helper functions for coordinate transformations
    Point3 transformToConical(const Point3& point, double cone_angle, double center_x, double center_y, double layer_height_mm);
    double calculateConicalLayerHeight(double radius, double cone_angle);
    
    // Function to adjust extrusion for conical layers
    void adjustExtrusion(ExtrusionLoop* loop, double scale_factor);

    // Nozzle geometry for collision detection
    double nozzle_tip_radius;
    double nozzle_cone_angle; // in degrees
    double nozzle_height; // Total height of the nozzle cone
    
    // Function to check for collisions between the nozzle and previous toolpaths
    bool checkForCollision(const Geometry::Point_3& nozzle_tip, double nozzle_tip_radius, double nozzle_cone_angle, double nozzle_height,
                           const std::vector<std::vector<Geometry::Point_3>>& previous_toolpaths);
    // Function to add new toolpath points to the collision detection system
    void addToolpathPoint(const Point3& point);

    // Data structure to store simplified toolpath points for collision detection
    std::vector<std::vector<Geometry::Point_3>> previous_toolpaths; // outer vector is layers, inner is points in the layer
    static constexpr size_t MAX_LAYERS_TO_CHECK = 3; // Maximum number of previous layers to check for collisions

    // Octree for collision detection
    Octree* toolpath_octree;
};

} // namespace Slic3r

Octree.hpp:

C++

#ifndef SLIC3R_OCTREE_HPP
#define SLIC3R_OCTREE_HPP

#include <vector>
#include "Geometry.hpp"
#include "BoundingBox.hpp"

namespace Slic3r {

    class Octree {
    public:
        Octree(const BoundingBox& bounds, int capacity = 4);
        ~Octree();

        void insert(const Geometry::Point_3& point);
        void queryRange(const Geometry::Point_3& center, double radius, std::vector<Geometry::Point_3>& result) const;
        void clear();

    private:
        struct Node {
            BoundingBox bounds;
            std::vector<Geometry::Point_3> points;
            Node* children[8]; // Eight children for an octree
            bool isLeaf;

            Node(const BoundingBox& b) : bounds(b), isLeaf(true) {
                for (int i = 0; i < 8; ++i) children[i] = nullptr;
            }
        };

        Node* root;
        int capacity; // Maximum number of points per node before subdividing

        void insertRecursive(Node* node, const Geometry::Point_3& point);
        void subdivide(Node* node);
        void queryRangeRecursive(Node* node, const Geometry::Point_3& center, double radius, std::vector<Geometry::Point_3>& result) const;
        void deleteNode(Node* node);
    };

} // namespace Slic3r

#endif // SLIC3R_OCTREE_HPP
Octree.cpp:

C++

#include "Octree.hpp"
#include <algorithm>

namespace Slic3r {

    Octree::Octree(const BoundingBox& bounds, int nodeCapacity) : capacity(nodeCapacity) {
        root = new Node(bounds);
    }

    Octree::~Octree() {
        deleteNode(root);
    }

    void Octree::deleteNode(Node* node) {
        if (node) {
            if (!node->isLeaf) {
                for (int i = 0; i < 8; ++i) {
                    deleteNode(node->children[i]);
                }
            }
            delete node;
        }
    }

    void Octree::insert(const Geometry::Point_3& point) {
        insertRecursive(root, point);
    }

    void Octree::insertRecursive(Node* node, const Geometry::Point_3& point) {
        if (!node->bounds.contains(Point(point.x(), point.y())))
            return; // Point is outside the bounds of the node

        if (node->isLeaf) {
            node->points.push_back(point);
            if (node->points.size() > capacity) {
                subdivide(node);
            }
        }
        else {
            // Recursively insert into the appropriate child node
            for (int i = 0; i < 8; ++i) {
                if (node->children[i]->bounds.contains(Point(point.x(), point.y()))) {
                    insertRecursive(node->children[i], point);
                    break;
                }
            }
        }
    }

    void Octree::subdivide(Node* node) {
        // Create eight children
        Vec3f half_size = (node->bounds.max - node->bounds.min) / 2.0f;
        for (int i = 0; i < 8; ++i) {
            Vec3f child_min = node->bounds.min;
            if ((i & 1) != 0) child_min.x() += half_size.x();
            if ((i & 2) != 0) child_min.y() += half_size.y();
            if ((i & 4) != 0) child_min.z() += half_size.z();
            node->children[i] = new Node(BoundingBox(child_min, child_min + half_size));
        }

        // Distribute points to children
        for (const Geometry::Point_3& p : node->points) {
            for (int i = 0; i < 8; ++i) {
                if (node->children[i]->bounds.contains(Point(p.x(), p.y()))) {
                    insertRecursive(node->children[i], p);
                    break;
                }
            }
        }

        node->points.clear();
        node->isLeaf = false;
    }

    void Octree::queryRange(const Geometry::Point_3& center, double radius, std::vector<Geometry::Point_3>& result) const {
        queryRangeRecursive(root, center, radius, result);
    }

    void Octree::queryRangeRecursive(Node* node, const Geometry::Point_3& center, double radius, std::vector<Geometry::Point_3>& result) const {
        // Check if the node's bounding box intersects the query sphere
        if (!node->bounds.intersectsSphere(Point(center.x(), center.y()), center.z(), radius)) {
            return; // No intersection
        }

        if (node->isLeaf) {
            // If it's a leaf node, check each point
            for (const Geometry::Point_3& p : node->points) {
                if (Geometry::distance(Point(center.x(), center.y()), Point(p.x(), p.y())) <= radius) {
                    result.push_back(p);
                }
            }
        }
        else {
            // If it's not a leaf node, recursively query the children
            for (int i = 0; i < 8; ++i) {
                queryRangeRecursive(node->children[i], center, radius, result);
            }
        }
    }

    void Octree::clear() {
        deleteNode(root);
        root = new Node(root->bounds); // Recreate the root node with the same bounds
    }

} // namespace Slic3r

#ifndef BOUNDINGBOX_HPP
#define BOUNDINGBOX_HPP

#include "Point.hpp"
#include "Vec.hpp"

namespace Slic3r {

class BoundingBox {
public:
    Point min;
    Point max;
    bool defined;

    BoundingBox();
    BoundingBox(const Point& min_pt, const Point& max_pt);
    BoundingBox(const Vec3f& min_pt, const Vec3f& max_pt);

    void merge(const Point& point);
    void merge(const Vec3f& point);
    void merge(const BoundingBox& other);

    bool contains(const Point& point) const;
    bool contains(const Vec3f& point) const;
    bool intersectsSphere(const Point& center, double z, double radius) const;

    Vec3f size() const;
    Point center() const;
};

} // namespace Slic3r

#endif // BOUNDINGBOX_HPP
BoundingBox.cpp:

C++

#include "BoundingBox.hpp"
#include <algorithm>
#include <limits>

namespace Slic3r {

BoundingBox::BoundingBox() : defined(false) {}

BoundingBox::BoundingBox(const Point& min_pt, const Point& max_pt)
    : min(min_pt), max(max_pt), defined(true) {}

BoundingBox::BoundingBox(const Vec3f& min_pt, const Vec3f& max_pt)
    : min(static_cast<coord_t>(min_pt.x()), static_cast<coord_t>(min_pt.y())),
      max(static_cast<coord_t>(max_pt.x()), static_cast<coord_t>(max_pt.y())),
      defined(true)
{
}

void BoundingBox::merge(const Point& point) {
    if (!defined) {
        min = point;
        max = point;
        defined = true;
    } else {
        min.x() = std::min(min.x(), point.x());
        min.y() = std::min(min.y(), point.y());
        max.x() = std::max(max.x(), point.x());
        max.y() = std::max(max.y(), point.y());
    }
}

void BoundingBox::merge(const Vec3f& point) {
    merge(Point(static_cast<coord_t>(point.x()), static_cast<coord_t>(point.y())));
}

void BoundingBox::merge(const BoundingBox& other) {
    if (!other.defined)
        return;
    if (!defined) {
        *this = other;
    } else {
        merge(other.min);
        merge(other.max);
    }
}

bool BoundingBox::contains(const Point& point) const {
    return defined &&
           point.x() >= min.x() && point.x() <= max.x() &&
           point.y() >= min.y() && point.y() <= max.y();
}

bool BoundingBox::contains(const Vec3f& point) const {
    return contains(Point(static_cast<coord_t>(point.x()), static_cast<coord_t>(point.y())));
}

bool BoundingBox::intersectsSphere(const Point& center, double z, double radius) const {
    // Check if the bounding box intersects with a sphere at a given z-height
    if (!defined)
        return false;

    // Find the closest point to the sphere's center on the bounding box
    Point closest_point;
    closest_point.x() = std::max(min.x(), std::min(center.x(), max.x()));
    closest_point.y() = std::max(min.y(), std::min(center.y(), max.y()));

    // Calculate the distance between the closest point and the sphere's center
    double distance_squared = std::pow(closest_point.x() - center.x(), 2) +
                              std::pow(closest_point.y() - center.y(), 2);

    // Check if the distance is less than or equal to the radius squared

2.0 Experimental Advanced. Lacks access to real-time info and some Gemini features.
C++

    return distance_squared <= std::pow(radius, 2);
}

Vec3f BoundingBox::size() const {
    return max - min;
}

Point BoundingBox::center() const {
    return Point((min.x() + max.x()) / 2, (min.y() + max.y()) / 2);
}

} // namespace Slic3r

Explanation of the Patch:

MainFrame.cpp/hpp: Adds a reload_print_settings method to MainFrame to force a reload of print settings, which is necessary to update the UI after changes.
PrintSettings.cpp/hpp:
Adds UI elements (checkboxes and text controls) for the conical slicing parameters:
enable_conical_slicing
cone_angle
cone_center_x
cone_center_y
nozzle_tip_radius
nozzle_cone_angle
nozzle_height
enable_path_smoothing
Binds these UI elements to the corresponding PrintConfig options.
Adds a reload_print_settings method to reload and refresh the print settings in the UI.
Tab.cpp/hpp: Adds a reload_print_settings method to the Tab class.
ConicalSlicer.hpp/cpp:
Defines the ConicalSlicer class, which handles the core conical slicing logic.
Implements member functions for coordinate transformation, layer height calculation, extrusion adjustment, collision detection, and adding toolpath points to the octree.
Integrates the Octree for collision detection.
Includes logic for segment splitting during collision handling.
Geometry.hpp/cpp:
Implements segmentConeIntersection using CGAL for accurate intersection calculations between a line segment and a cone.
Includes error handling using try-catch blocks.
Print.hpp/cpp:
Integrates the ConicalSlicer into the main slicing process.
Conditionally calls sliceLayerConically based on the enable_conical_slicing flag.
Includes logic to handle the use_planar_slicing flag set by ConicalSlicer.
PrintConfig.hpp/cpp:
Defines configuration options for the new conical slicing parameters.
Sets default values for these options.
Octree.hpp/cpp: Provides a basic Octree implementation for spatial indexing to speed up collision detection.
BoundingBox.hpp/cpp: Provides BoundingBox class, which is used by the Octree.
Smoothing.hpp/cpp: Implements path smoothing using the TinySpline library.
CMakeLists.txt:
Adds the new .cpp and .hpp files to the list of source files to be compiled.
Includes directives to find and link the CGAL and Boost libraries.
To apply this patch:

Save the above code as 0001-conical-slicing.patch in your patches directory.
Use the setup.py script to build OrcaSlicer. The script will automatically apply the patch during the build process.
Alternatively, apply the patch manually:
Bash

cd <path_to_your_OrcaSlicer_fork>
git apply ../patches/0001-conical-slicing.patch
This patch addresses all the major points we've discussed and should provide a solid foundation for your conical slicing feature in OrcaSlicer. Remember to test thoroughly and refine the implementation as needed.

Geometry.cpp:

C++

#include "Geometry.hpp"
#include <cmath>
#include <algorithm>

// Include CGAL headers
#include <CGAL/Exact_predicates_inexact_constructions_kernel.h>
#include <CGAL/Segment_3.h>
#include <CGAL/intersection.h>
#include <CGAL/Origin.h>
#include "PrintConfig.hpp"

namespace Slic3r {
namespace Geometry {

// ... other functions ...

bool segmentConeIntersection(const Point3& p1, const Point3& p2, const Point3& nozzle_tip,
    double nozzle_tip_radius, double nozzle_cone_angle, double nozzle_height) {
    try {
        // Create CGAL points for the segment
        K::Point_3 cp1(p1.x(), p1.y(), p1.z());
        K::Point_3 cp2(p2.x(), p2.y(), p2.z());
        Segment_3 segment(cp1, cp2);

        // Create CGAL points for the nozzle cone
        K::Point_3 c_nozzle_tip(nozzle_tip.x(), nozzle_tip.y(), nozzle_tip.z());

        // Calculate the apex of the cone (where the tip would be if the cone continued)
        FT cone_height_to_apex = nozzle_tip_radius / tan(deg2rad(nozzle_cone_angle / 2.0));

        // Define the direction vector of the cone axis (pointing upwards from the tip)
        Vector_3 cone_axis_direction(0, 0, 1);

        // Calculate the apex point of the cone
        K::Point_3 apex = c_nozzle_tip - cone_axis_direction * cone_height_to_apex;

        // Create a CGAL Cone
        // The radius at the base of the cone needs to be calculated considering the nozzle height
        FT base_radius = (nozzle_tip_radius + nozzle_height * tan(deg2rad(nozzle_cone_angle / 2.0)));

        // Create a CGAL Cone
        K::Cone_3 cone(apex, cone_axis_direction, CGAL::square(base_radius), cone_height_to_apex);
        
        // Check for intersection
        auto intersection_result = CGAL::intersection(segment, cone);

        // Check if an intersection occurred
        if (intersection_result) {
            // Further check based on the type of intersection
            if (const Segment_3* segment_result = boost::get<Segment_3>(&*intersection_result)) {
                // Intersection is a segment
                return true;
            }
            else if (const Point_3* point_result = boost::get<Point_3>(&*intersection_result)) {
                // Intersection is a point
                return true;
            }
        }
    }
    catch (const CGAL::Precondition_exception& e) {
        std::cerr << "CGAL Precondition Exception in segmentConeIntersection: " << e.what() << std::endl;
        // Handle the error (e.g., log, switch to planar slicing, etc.)
        return false;
    }
    catch (const std::exception& e) {
        std::cerr << "Exception in segmentConeIntersection: " << e.what() << std::endl;
        // Handle the error
        return false;
    }

    return false;
}

} // namespace Geometry
} // namespace Slic3r

Problem: vcpkg failed to install via Chocolatey
Solution: Install vcpkg manually instead. Here's how:

1. Open PowerShell as Admin

2. Install vcpkg Manually

🚨 Let's Fix the Python Build Error in vcpkg - Step-by-Step Solution

1. Root Cause Analysis
The error occurs because vcpkg is trying to build Python 3.11 from source but is missing required Windows SDK components. This is not needed for OrcaSlicer - we can bypass it!

2. Quick Fix - Skip Python Build
Run these commands in PowerShell as Admin:

powershell
Copy
# Uninstall broken Python attempt
cd C:\vcpkg
.\vcpkg remove python3 --triplet x64-windows

# Install dependencies WITHOUT Python
.\vcpkg install cgal boost --triplet x64-windows --skip-packages=python3
3. Alternative Solution - Use Prebuilt Python
If you still need Python (for other features):

powershell
Copy
# Install Windows 10 SDK first
choco install -y windows-sdk-10.1

# Then retry vcpkg install
.\vcpkg install python3 --triplet x64-windows
4. Verify Successful Installation
Check for these key files:

powershell
Copy
# Should return paths if successful
Test-Path C:\vcpkg\installed\x64-windows\include\CGAL\*.hpp
Test-Path C:\vcpkg\installed\x64-windows\lib\boost_*.lib
5. Resume OrcaSlicer Build
powershell
Copy
cd C:\Your\OrcaSlicer\Build\Folder
rm -Recurse -Force build  # Delete old build
mkdir build
cd build

# Configure with fixed settings
cmake .. -G "Visual Studio 17 2022" -A x64 `
-DCMAKE_TOOLCHAIN_FILE="C:/vcpkg/scripts/buildsystems/vcpkg.cmake" `
-DVCPKG_TARGET_TRIPLET=x64-windows

# Build!
cmake --build . --config Release
